!  Average Annual Spot Prices by State ($/MMBtu), need to be converted to 1987$/Mcf
!      Used to set wellhead prices by subtracting gathering charges specified by OGDIST regions 
!      Source NGI spot prices, most are averages of more than one price.  When no price available assumed a difference between a neighboring state.
!      Details in David Fritsch spreadsheet
!Re-calclulated in the code as a straight average of monthly spot price data from the next table
!Added in international and border point annual spot prices (KDL, 6/30/17)
